5682:   ISIdentity(isrow,&row_identity);
5683:   ISIdentity(iscol,&col_identity);
5684:   both_identity = (PetscTruth) (row_identity && col_identity);
5685: 
5686:   if (!levels && both_identity) {
5687:     /* special case: ilu(0) with natural ordering */
5688:     MatILUFactorSymbolic_SeqBAIJ_ilu0(fact,A,isrow,iscol,info);
5689:     MatSeqBAIJSetNumericFactorization(fact,both_identity);

5691:     fact->factor = MAT_FACTOR_ILU;
5692:     (fact)->info.factor_mallocs    = 0;
5693:     (fact)->info.fill_ratio_given  = info->fill;
5694:     (fact)->info.fill_ratio_needed = 1.0;
5695:     b                = (Mat_SeqBAIJ*)(fact)->data;
5696:     b->row           = isrow;
5697:     b->col           = iscol;
5698:     b->icol          = isicol;
5699:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)isrow);
5700:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)iscol);
5701:     b->pivotinblocks = (info->pivotinblocks) ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
5702:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*bs*sizeof(PetscScalar),&b->solve_work);
5703:     return(0);
5704:   }
5705: 
5706:   ISGetIndices(isrow,&r);
5707:   ISGetIndices(isicol,&ic);
5708: 
5709:   /* get new row pointers */
5710:   PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&bi);
5711:   bi[0] = 0;
5712:   /* bdiag is location of diagonal in factor */
5713:   PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&bdiag);
5714:   bdiag[0]  = 0;

5716:   PetscMalloc2(n,PetscInt*,&bj_ptr,n,PetscInt*,&bjlvl_ptr);

5718:   /* create a linked list for storing column indices of the active row */
5719:   nlnk = n + 1;
5720:   PetscIncompleteLLCreate(n,n,nlnk,lnk,lnk_lvl,lnkbt);
5721: 
5722:   /* initial FreeSpace size is f*(ai[n]+1) */
5723:   PetscFreeSpaceGet((PetscInt)(f*(ai[n]+1)),&free_space);
5724:   current_space = free_space;
5725:   PetscFreeSpaceGet((PetscInt)(f*(ai[n]+1)),&free_space_lvl);
5726:   current_space_lvl = free_space_lvl;
5727: 
5728:   for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
5729:     nzi = 0;
5730:     /* copy current row into linked list */
5731:     nnz  = ai[r[i]+1] - ai[r[i]];
5732:     if (!nnz) SETERRQ2(PETSC_ERR_MAT_LU_ZRPVT,"Empty row in matrix: row in original ordering %D in permuted ordering %D",r[i],i);
5733:     cols = aj + ai[r[i]];
5734:     lnk[i] = -1; /* marker to indicate if diagonal exists */
5735:     PetscIncompleteLLInit(nnz,cols,n,ic,nlnk,lnk,lnk_lvl,lnkbt);
5736:     nzi += nlnk;

5738:     /* make sure diagonal entry is included */
5739:     if (diagonal_fill && lnk[i] == -1) {
5740:       fm = n;
5741:       while (lnk[fm] < i) fm = lnk[fm];
5742:       lnk[i]     = lnk[fm]; /* insert diagonal into linked list */
5743:       lnk[fm]    = i;
5744:       lnk_lvl[i] = 0;
5745:       nzi++; dcount++;
5746:     }

5748:     /* add pivot rows into the active row */
5749:     nzbd = 0;
5750:     prow = lnk[n];
5751:     while (prow < i) {
5752:       nnz      = bdiag[prow];
5753:       cols     = bj_ptr[prow] + nnz + 1;
5754:       cols_lvl = bjlvl_ptr[prow] + nnz + 1;
5755:       nnz      = bi[prow+1] - bi[prow] - nnz - 1;
5756:       PetscILULLAddSorted(nnz,cols,levels,cols_lvl,prow,nlnk,lnk,lnk_lvl,lnkbt,prow);
5757:       nzi += nlnk;
5758:       prow = lnk[prow];
5759:       nzbd++;
5760:     }
5761:     bdiag[i] = nzbd;
5762:     bi[i+1]  = bi[i] + nzi;

5764:     /* if free space is not available, make more free space */
5765:     if (current_space->local_remaining<nzi) {
5766:       nnz = 2*nzi*(n - i); /* estimated and max additional space needed */
5767:       PetscFreeSpaceGet(nnz,&current_space);
5768:       PetscFreeSpaceGet(nnz,&current_space_lvl);
5769:       reallocs++;
5770:     }

5772:     /* copy data into free_space and free_space_lvl, then initialize lnk */
5773:     PetscIncompleteLLClean(n,n,nzi,lnk,lnk_lvl,current_space->array,current_space_lvl->array,lnkbt);
5774:     bj_ptr[i]    = current_space->array;
5775:     bjlvl_ptr[i] = current_space_lvl->array;

5777:     /* make sure the active row i has diagonal entry */
5778:     if (*(bj_ptr[i]+bdiag[i]) != i) {
5779:       SETERRQ1(PETSC_ERR_MAT_LU_ZRPVT,"Row %D has missing diagonal in factored matrix\n\
5780:     try running with -pc_factor_nonzeros_along_diagonal or -pc_factor_diagonal_fill",i);
5781:     }

5783:     current_space->array           += nzi;
5784:     current_space->local_used      += nzi;
5785:     current_space->local_remaining -= nzi;
5786:     current_space_lvl->array           += nzi;
5787:     current_space_lvl->local_used      += nzi;
5788:     current_space_lvl->local_remaining -= nzi;
5789:   }
5790: 
5791:   ISRestoreIndices(isrow,&r);
5792:   ISRestoreIndices(isicol,&ic);

5794:   /* destroy list of free space and other temporary arrays */
5795:   PetscMalloc((bi[n]+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&bj);
5796: 
5797:   /* copy free_space into bj and free free_space; set bi, bj, bdiag in new datastructure; */
5798:   PetscFreeSpaceContiguous_LU(&free_space,bj,n,bi,bdiag);
5799: 
5800:   PetscIncompleteLLDestroy(lnk,lnkbt);
5801:   PetscFreeSpaceDestroy(free_space_lvl);
5802:   PetscFree2(bj_ptr,bjlvl_ptr);

5804: #if defined(PETSC_USE_INFO)
5805:   {
5806:     PetscReal af = ((PetscReal)(bdiag[0]+1))/((PetscReal)ai[n]);
5807:     PetscInfo3(A,"Reallocs %D Fill ratio:given %G needed %G\n",reallocs,f,af);
5808:     PetscInfo1(A,"Run with -[sub_]pc_factor_fill %G or use \n",af);
5809:     PetscInfo1(A,"PCFactorSetFill([sub]pc,%G);\n",af);
5810:     PetscInfo(A,"for best performance.\n");
5811:     if (diagonal_fill) {
5812:       PetscInfo1(A,"Detected and replaced %D missing diagonals",dcount);
5813:     }
5814:   }
5815: #endif

5817:   /* put together the new matrix */
5818:   MatSeqBAIJSetPreallocation_SeqBAIJ(fact,bs,MAT_SKIP_ALLOCATION,PETSC_NULL);
5819:   PetscLogObjectParent(fact,isicol);
5820:   b = (Mat_SeqBAIJ*)(fact)->data;
5821:   b->free_a       = PETSC_TRUE;
5822:   b->free_ij      = PETSC_TRUE;
5823:   b->singlemalloc = PETSC_FALSE;
5824:   PetscMalloc( (bs2*(bdiag[0]+1) )*sizeof(MatScalar),&b->a);
5825:   b->j          = bj;
5826:   b->i          = bi;
5827:   b->diag       = bdiag;
5828:   b->free_diag  = PETSC_TRUE;
5829:   b->ilen       = 0;
5830:   b->imax       = 0;
5831:   b->row        = isrow;
5832:   b->col        = iscol;
5833:   PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)isrow);
5834:   PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)iscol);
5835:   b->icol       = isicol;
5836:   PetscMalloc((bs*n+bs)*sizeof(PetscScalar),&b->solve_work);
5837:   /* In b structure:  Free imax, ilen, old a, old j.  
5838:      Allocate bdiag, solve_work, new a, new j */
5839:   PetscLogObjectMemory(fact,(bdiag[0]+1) * (sizeof(PetscInt)+bs2*sizeof(PetscScalar)));
5840:   b->maxnz = b->nz = bdiag[0]+1;
5841:   fact->info.factor_mallocs    = reallocs;
5842:   fact->info.fill_ratio_given  = f;
5843:   fact->info.fill_ratio_needed = ((PetscReal)(bdiag[0]+1))/((PetscReal)ai[n]);
5844:   MatSeqBAIJSetNumericFactorization(fact,both_identity);
5845:   return(0);
5846: }

5848: /*
5849:      This code is virtually identical to MatILUFactorSymbolic_SeqAIJ
5850:    except that the data structure of Mat_SeqAIJ is slightly different.
5851:    Not a good example of code reuse.
5852: */
5855: PetscErrorCode MatILUFactorSymbolic_SeqBAIJ_inplace(Mat fact,Mat A,IS isrow,IS iscol,const MatFactorInfo *info)
5856: {
5857:   Mat_SeqBAIJ    *a = (Mat_SeqBAIJ*)A->data,*b;
5858:   IS             isicol;
5860:   const PetscInt *r,*ic,*ai = a->i,*aj = a->j,*xi;
5861:   PetscInt       prow,n = a->mbs,*ainew,*ajnew,jmax,*fill,nz,*im,*ajfill,*flev,*xitmp;
5862:   PetscInt       *dloc,idx,row,m,fm,nzf,nzi,reallocate = 0,dcount = 0;
5863:   PetscInt       incrlev,nnz,i,bs = A->rmap->bs,bs2 = a->bs2,levels,diagonal_fill,dd;
5864:   PetscTruth     col_identity,row_identity,both_identity,flg;
5865:   PetscReal      f;

5868:   MatMissingDiagonal_SeqBAIJ(A,&flg,&dd);
5869:   if (flg) SETERRQ1(PETSC_ERR_ARG_WRONGSTATE,"Matrix A is missing diagonal entry in row %D",dd);
5870: 
5871:   f             = info->fill;
5872:   levels        = (PetscInt)info->levels;
5873:   diagonal_fill = (PetscInt)info->diagonal_fill;
5874:   ISInvertPermutation(iscol,PETSC_DECIDE,&isicol);

5876:   ISIdentity(isrow,&row_identity);
5877:   ISIdentity(iscol,&col_identity);
5878:   both_identity = (PetscTruth) (row_identity && col_identity);

5880:   if (!levels && both_identity) {  /* special case copy the nonzero structure */
5881:     MatDuplicateNoCreate_SeqBAIJ(fact,A,MAT_DO_NOT_COPY_VALUES,PETSC_TRUE);
5882:     MatSeqBAIJSetNumericFactorization_inplace(fact,both_identity);

5884:     fact->factor = MAT_FACTOR_ILU;
5885:     b            = (Mat_SeqBAIJ*)fact->data;
5886:     b->row       = isrow;
5887:     b->col       = iscol;
5888:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)isrow);
5889:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)iscol);
5890:     b->icol      = isicol;
5891:     b->pivotinblocks = (info->pivotinblocks) ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
5892:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*bs*sizeof(PetscScalar),&b->solve_work);
5893:     return(0);
5894:   }

5896:   /* general case perform the symbolic factorization */
5897:     ISGetIndices(isrow,&r);
5898:     ISGetIndices(isicol,&ic);

5900:     /* get new row pointers */
5901:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&ainew);
5902:     ainew[0] = 0;
5903:     /* don't know how many column pointers are needed so estimate */
5904:     jmax = (PetscInt)(f*ai[n] + 1);
5905:     PetscMalloc((jmax)*sizeof(PetscInt),&ajnew);
5906:     /* ajfill is level of fill for each fill entry */
5907:     PetscMalloc((jmax)*sizeof(PetscInt),&ajfill);
5908:     /* fill is a linked list of nonzeros in active row */
5909:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&fill);
5910:     /* im is level for each filled value */
5911:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&im);
5912:     /* dloc is location of diagonal in factor */
5913:     PetscMalloc((n+1)*sizeof(PetscInt),&dloc);
5914:     dloc[0]  = 0;
5915:     for (prow=0; prow<n; prow++) {

5917:       /* copy prow into linked list */
5918:       nzf        = nz  = ai[r[prow]+1] - ai[r[prow]];
5919:       if (!nz) SETERRQ2(PETSC_ERR_MAT_LU_ZRPVT,"Empty row in matrix: row in original ordering %D in permuted ordering %D",r[prow],prow);
5920:       xi         = aj + ai[r[prow]];
5921:       fill[n]    = n;
5922:       fill[prow] = -1; /* marker for diagonal entry */
5923:       while (nz--) {
5924:         fm  = n;
5925:         idx = ic[*xi++];
5926:         do {
5927:           m  = fm;
5928:           fm = fill[m];
5929:         } while (fm < idx);
5930:         fill[m]   = idx;
5931:         fill[idx] = fm;
5932:         im[idx]   = 0;
5933:       }

5935:       /* make sure diagonal entry is included */
5936:       if (diagonal_fill && fill[prow] == -1) {
5937:         fm = n;
5938:         while (fill[fm] < prow) fm = fill[fm];
5939:         fill[prow] = fill[fm];  /* insert diagonal into linked list */
5940:         fill[fm]   = prow;
5941:         im[prow]   = 0;
5942:         nzf++;
5943:         dcount++;
5944:       }

5946:       nzi = 0;
5947:       row = fill[n];
5948:       while (row < prow) {
5949:         incrlev = im[row] + 1;
5950:         nz      = dloc[row];
5951:         xi      = ajnew  + ainew[row] + nz + 1;
5952:         flev    = ajfill + ainew[row] + nz + 1;
5953:         nnz     = ainew[row+1] - ainew[row] - nz - 1;
5954:         fm      = row;
5955:         while (nnz-- > 0) {
5956:           idx = *xi++;
5957:           if (*flev + incrlev > levels) {
5958:             flev++;
5959:             continue;
5960:           }
5961:           do {
5962:             m  = fm;
5963:             fm = fill[m];
5964:           } while (fm < idx);
5965:           if (fm != idx) {
5966:             im[idx]   = *flev + incrlev;
5967:             fill[m]   = idx;
5968:             fill[idx] = fm;
5969:             fm        = idx;
5970:             nzf++;
5971:           } else {
5972:             if (im[idx] > *flev + incrlev) im[idx] = *flev+incrlev;
5973:           }
5974:           flev++;
5975:         }
5976:         row = fill[row];
5977:         nzi++;
5978:       }
5979:       /* copy new filled row into permanent storage */
5980:       ainew[prow+1] = ainew[prow] + nzf;
5981:       if (ainew[prow+1] > jmax) {

5983:         /* estimate how much additional space we will need */
5984:         /* use the strategy suggested by David Hysom <hysom@perch-t.icase.edu> */
5985:         /* just double the memory each time */
5986:         PetscInt maxadd = jmax;
5987:         /* maxadd = (int)(((f*ai[n]+1)*(n-prow+5))/n); */
5988:         if (maxadd < nzf) maxadd = (n-prow)*(nzf+1);
5989:         jmax += maxadd;

5991:         /* allocate a longer ajnew and ajfill */
5992:         PetscMalloc(jmax*sizeof(PetscInt),&xitmp);
5993:         PetscMemcpy(xitmp,ajnew,ainew[prow]*sizeof(PetscInt));
5994:         PetscFree(ajnew);
5995:         ajnew = xitmp;
5996:         PetscMalloc(jmax*sizeof(PetscInt),&xitmp);
5997:         PetscMemcpy(xitmp,ajfill,ainew[prow]*sizeof(PetscInt));
5998:         PetscFree(ajfill);
5999:         ajfill = xitmp;
6000:         reallocate++; /* count how many reallocations are needed */
6001:       }
6002:       xitmp       = ajnew + ainew[prow];
6003:       flev        = ajfill + ainew[prow];
6004:       dloc[prow]  = nzi;
6005:       fm          = fill[n];
6006:       while (nzf--) {
6007:         *xitmp++ = fm;
6008:         *flev++ = im[fm];
6009:         fm      = fill[fm];
6010:       }
6011:       /* make sure row has diagonal entry */
6012:       if (ajnew[ainew[prow]+dloc[prow]] != prow) {
6013:         SETERRQ1(PETSC_ERR_MAT_LU_ZRPVT,"Row %D has missing diagonal in factored matrix\n\
6014:     try running with -pc_factor_nonzeros_along_diagonal or -pc_factor_diagonal_fill",prow);
6015:       }
6016:     }
6017:     PetscFree(ajfill);
6018:     ISRestoreIndices(isrow,&r);
6019:     ISRestoreIndices(isicol,&ic);
6020:     PetscFree(fill);
6021:     PetscFree(im);

6023: #if defined(PETSC_USE_INFO)
6024:     {
6025:       PetscReal af = ((PetscReal)ainew[n])/((PetscReal)ai[n]);
6026:       PetscInfo3(A,"Reallocs %D Fill ratio:given %G needed %G\n",reallocate,f,af);
6027:       PetscInfo1(A,"Run with -pc_factor_fill %G or use \n",af);
6028:       PetscInfo1(A,"PCFactorSetFill(pc,%G);\n",af);
6029:       PetscInfo(A,"for best performance.\n");
6030:       if (diagonal_fill) {
6031:         PetscInfo1(A,"Detected and replaced %D missing diagonals\n",dcount);
6032:       }
6033:     }
6034: #endif

6036:     /* put together the new matrix */
6037:     MatSeqBAIJSetPreallocation_SeqBAIJ(fact,bs,MAT_SKIP_ALLOCATION,PETSC_NULL);
6038:     PetscLogObjectParent(fact,isicol);
6039:     b    = (Mat_SeqBAIJ*)fact->data;
6040:     b->free_a       = PETSC_TRUE;
6041:     b->free_ij      = PETSC_TRUE;
6042:     b->singlemalloc = PETSC_FALSE;
6043:     PetscMalloc(bs2*ainew[n]*sizeof(MatScalar),&b->a);
6044:     b->j          = ajnew;
6045:     b->i          = ainew;
6046:     for (i=0; i<n; i++) dloc[i] += ainew[i];
6047:     b->diag       = dloc;
6048:     b->free_diag  = PETSC_TRUE;
6049:     b->ilen       = 0;
6050:     b->imax       = 0;
6051:     b->row        = isrow;
6052:     b->col        = iscol;
6053:     b->pivotinblocks = (info->pivotinblocks) ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
6054:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)isrow);
6055:     PetscObjectReference((PetscObject)iscol);
6056:     b->icol       = isicol;
6057:     PetscMalloc((bs*n+bs)*sizeof(PetscScalar),&b->solve_work);
6058:     /* In b structure:  Free imax, ilen, old a, old j.  
6059:        Allocate dloc, solve_work, new a, new j */
6060:     PetscLogObjectMemory(fact,(ainew[n]-n)*(sizeof(PetscInt))+bs2*ainew[n]*sizeof(PetscScalar));
6061:     b->maxnz          = b->nz = ainew[n];

6063:     fact->info.factor_mallocs    = reallocate;
6064:     fact->info.fill_ratio_given  = f;
6065:     fact->info.fill_ratio_needed = ((PetscReal)ainew[n])/((PetscReal)ai[prow]);

6067:   MatSeqBAIJSetNumericFactorization_inplace(fact,both_identity);
6068:   return(0);
6069: }

6073: PetscErrorCode MatSetUnfactored_SeqBAIJ_4_NaturalOrdering_SSE(Mat A)
6074: {
6075:   /* Mat_SeqBAIJ *a = (Mat_SeqBAIJ *)A->data; */
6076:   /* int i,*AJ=a->j,nz=a->nz; */
6078:   /* Undo Column scaling */
6079: /*    while (nz--) { */
6080: /*      AJ[i] = AJ[i]/4; */
6081: /*    } */
6082:   /* This should really invoke a push/pop logic, but we don't have that yet. */
6083:   A->ops->setunfactored = PETSC_NULL;
6084:   return(0);
6085: }

6089: PetscErrorCode MatSetUnfactored_SeqBAIJ_4_NaturalOrdering_SSE_usj(Mat A)
6090: {
6091:   Mat_SeqBAIJ    *a = (Mat_SeqBAIJ *)A->data;
6092:   PetscInt       *AJ=a->j,nz=a->nz;
6093:   unsigned short *aj=(unsigned short *)AJ;
6095:   /* Is this really necessary? */
6096:   while (nz--) {
6097:     AJ[nz] = (int)((unsigned int)aj[nz]); /* First extend, then convert to signed. */
6098:   }
6099:   A->ops->setunfactored = PETSC_NULL;
6100:   return(0);
6101: }
